<article about="/home-page" typeof="sioc:Item foaf:Document" class="node node-homepage node-published node-not-promoted node-not-sticky author-admin even clearfix" id="node-homepage-16219">
<section id="section-1b" class="carousel-section home-section">
<div class="container-12">
<div class="carousel-intro grid-6">
<div class="carousel-text">
<div class="field field-name-field-introduction field-type-text-long field-label-hidden">
<h1>Making Teaching Better</h1>
<p>We are an independent non-profit organisation committed to world-class teaching in higher education. We work in partnership with institutions and individuals in higher education supporting student success. The Higher Education Academy brings the sector together to collaborate, and share teaching strategies and practice. <a href="about-us">Learn more about HEA &gt;</a></p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="clearfix"></div>
</div>
<div class="clearfix"></div>
<div class="hea-box-container-2">
<div class="grid-4 individual-box">
<div class="hea-box-padding">
<div class="hea-box-matchheight">
<div class="field field-name-field-individuals-box field-type-text-long field-label-hidden">
<h2><a href="individuals" style="border-bottom-color: currentColor; border-bottom-width: medium; border-bottom-style: none;"><span style="color:rgb(247, 148, 30)">For You</span></a></h2>
<h3><a href="individuals" style="border-bottom-color: currentColor; border-bottom-width: medium; border-bottom-style: none;"><span style="color:rgb(247, 148, 30)">Seeking professional career development</span></a></h3>
<p>Explore a comprehensive range of services specifically designed to support you in your career, including <a href="fellowship">Fellowship</a>, <a href="training-events">Training and Events</a>, networking, <a href="https://www.heacademy.ac.uk/individuals/communities-of-practice">communities</a> and CPD tailored to individual <a href="disciplines">Disciplines</a>.</p>
</div>
<div class="clearfix"></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="grid-4 institution-box">
<div class="hea-box-padding">
<div class="hea-box-matchheight">
<div class="field field-name-field-institutions-box field-type-text-long field-label-hidden">
<h2><a href="individuals" style="border-bottom-color: currentColor; border-bottom-width: medium; border-bottom-style: none;"><span style="color:rgb(59, 61, 62)">For Your Institution</span></a></h2>
<h3><a href="institutions" style="border-bottom-color: currentColor; border-bottom-width: medium; border-bottom-style: none;"><span style="color:rgb(59, 61, 62)">To help deliver strategic objectives</span></a></h3>
<p><span style="color:rgb(59, 61, 62)">We work in partnership with institutions to resolve strategic challenges such as <a href="https://www.heacademy.ac.uk/institutions/consultancy/student-retention">retention</a>, <a href="services/consultancy/assessment-feedback">assessment</a>, and <a href="services/consultancy/employability">employability</a>, and to support 'workforce development'. Find out more about <a href="https://www.heacademy.ac.uk/institutions/subscription">Subscription</a>, <a href="services/accreditation">Accreditation</a> &amp; the <a href="ukpsf">UKPSF</a>, <a href="services/consultancy">Consultancy Services</a>, <a href="institutions/surveys">Surveys</a>, and <a href="https://www.international.heacademy.ac.uk/">International Services</a>.</span></p>
</div>
<div class="clearfix"></div>
</div>
